10a6(1): khyab pa gang la// de nyid mtha' dbus las 'das pa'o// he ni rgyu dang bral ba ste// ru ni mtshan ma'i gzugs las 'das// ka ni sku la mtshon dang bral// snying po rang bzhin gsung dang gsung // he ni chos sku mtshon dang / 
10a7(1): bral// ru ni longs spyod chen po ste// ka ni sna tshogs sprul pa'i sku// sku gsum lhun grub rtsol ba med// chos nyid smon lam thugs rje yin// dang khro shugs dang bcas pa ni// thugs rje byin brlabs bcas po nyid// 
10b1(1): byams dang sdang dang chags khro gnyis// yul dang bcas pa de bzhin 'gyur// gang du gang la snang ba// las dang thugs rje thabs 'brel pas// byin brlabs ye shes lhun rdzogs ni// dpag bsam nor bur gnas// dpag med
10b2(1): rim pa chos kyi dbyings// ye shes lnga'i ngo bo las// gdul bya'i blo ni rim pa bzhin// khrag 'thung lnga'i ngo bor gnas// sku ni snang ba thams cad de// gsung ni brjod pa kun nyid de// dran rtogs thugs la dbyer med pa// ma 
10b3(1): lus sku gsung thugs la rdzogs// kun gyi rang bzhin de nyid de// rgyu 'bras mtshon pa kun gyi stong // gang de de nyid rang snang ba// chu la chu bur snang ba ltar// ma bcos phyag brgya chen por gnas// sna tshogs phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid de//

10b5(1): las 'byung ba'i chos ma yin// dpal ldan ye shes he ru ka/ thabs chen mdzad pa kun gyi gnas// gsang ba'i gsang ba thugs// mkha' la dri med gsal ba ltar// skye med dbyings las phyag rgyar gsal// las dang ting 'dzin 
10b6(1): ye shes dang // yid kyi rnam par 'phrul pa mchog/ ji srid rnam rtog gnas kyi bar// de srid phyag rgya'i gnas mchog ste// gang dang 'tsham par gang snang ba// phyag rgya'i dkyil 'khor grangs las 'das// kun gyi gzhi rtsa snying po nyid//

11a1(1): bzhin// ma nor thabs dang ldan pa yis// skyes ldan dag pa'i skyes bu la// man ngag legs par bstan pa yis// gsang ba 'dzin pa'i rgyal por 'gyur ces gsungs so// dpal he ru ka 'dus pa'i rgyud chen po las/

11a3(1): med kyang // dman pas dam pa'i lta ba rtogs dga' bas// bdag cag rnams la rgya cher bshad du gsol// ces gsol ba las/ bcom ldan 'das ye shes thams cad kyi rgyal po nges 'di skad ces gsungs so// chos rnams ma

11a5(1): pa'i ngang du rang bzhin 'dus// dbyings dang ye shes thabs dang shes rab kyang // de nyid chen po'i nga du dbyer med pas// ma bcos chos dbyings brdal ba chen po la// sgro skur yin min dpyod dang rtog pa med// dam pa'i rang bzhin thabs 
11a6(1): kyis gang rtogs pa// chos rnams kun gyi rang bzhin dus gcig rtogs// gzhi rtsa kun gyis rang bzhin du dus gcig rtogs// gzhi rtsa kun 'das nam mkha'i rang bzhin la// blon pos ltas pas rang bzhin che tshad ltar// sems nyid mtha'

12a1(1): 'khor ba'i 'jigs bral mya ngan 'das smon med// gdod nas dag pa nam mkha'i rang bzhin la// mthong dang ma mthong blo bur rtog pa'i chos// dam pa'i don la mthong zhing gsal rtogs na// mthong dang ma mthong
